master than Windows.\u003c/strong\u003e Sometimes it's not user-friendly, and following an outdated tutorial may break the operating system.\u003cbr\u003e\nThere is no centralized software repository, except for the \u003ccode\u003eapt\u003c/code\u003e repositories which lack many desktop applications.\u003cbr\u003e\nSurely there is a better way! \u003cstrong\u003eThere is.\u003c/strong\u003e\u003cbr\u003e\nIntroducing Pi-Apps, a well-maintained collection of app installation-scripts that you can run with \u003cstrong\u003eone click\u003c/strong\u003e.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003ePi-Apps now serves \u003cstrong\u003eover 1,000,000 people\u003c/strong\u003e and hosts \u003ca Pi-Apps?\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cblockquote\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eFor a long time I have been saddened by how difficult it is to install software on Linux. In that regard, nearly all other operating systems put us to shame.\u003cbr\u003e\nHow will people discover useful, free software?\u003cbr\u003e\nMost people \u003cstrong\u003edon't\u003c/strong\u003e.\u003cbr\u003e\nOne day I realized: Why not make a collection of scripts to install popular apps? This would save so much time, and makes it much easier to use a Raspberry Pi as a daily, desktop computer solution.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/blockquote\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eHow long did it take to program this?\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cblockquote\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eWhy would you think it's not still under development? \u003cbr\u003e\nPi-Apps took around 14 days to lay the groundwork, and ever since then it has been continually, and exponentially, improved. I (Botspot) am not the sole programmer anymore - \u003ca href=\"https://github.com/Botspot/pi-apps/graphs/contributors\"\u003eothers\u003c/a\u003e have stepped in and made improvements too.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/blockquote\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eIs Pi-Apps free?\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cblockquote\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eAbsolutely! \u003ca href=\"https://github.com/sponsors/botspot\"\u003eDonations are welcome\u003c/a\u003e, but Pi-Apps itself will always be free and <p align="center" dir="auto">The most popular app store for Raspberry Pi computers. 100% free, open-source and written in shell scripts.

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Introduction</h2><a id="user-content-introduction" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Introduction" href="#introduction"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Let's be honest: <strong>ARM Linux is harder to master than Windows.</strong> Sometimes it's not user-friendly, and following an outdated tutorial may break the operating system.<br>
There is no centralized software repository, except for the <code>apt</code> repositories which lack many desktop applications.<br>
Surely there is a better way! <strong>There is.</strong><br>
Introducing Pi-Apps, a well-maintained collection of app installation-scripts that you can run with <strong>one click</strong>.</p>
<p dir="auto">Pi-Apps now serves <strong>over 1,000,000 people</strong> and hosts <a href="https://pi-apps.io/wiki/getting-started/apps-list/" rel="nofollow">over 200 apps</a>.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Install Pi-Apps</h2><a id="user-content-install-pi-apps" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Install Pi-Apps" href="#install-pi-apps"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Open a terminal and run this command:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="wget -qO- https://raw.githubusercontent.com/Botspot/pi-apps/master/install | bash"><pre>wget -qO- https://raw.githubusercontent.com/Botspot/pi-apps/master/install <span class="pl-k">|</span> bash</pre></div>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/Botspot/pi-apps/blob/master/icons/screenshots/main%20window.png?raw=true"><img src="/Botspot/pi-apps/raw/master/icons/screenshots/main%20window.png?raw=true" align="right" height="270px" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Supported systems:</h3><a id="user-content-supported-systems" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Supported systems:" href="#supported-systems"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Raspberry Pi <a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/a3e0767e9f766cbaf33956f988f77b971bd6ae1af5f4b88592d683a34bb9f8b5/68747470733a2f2f70692d617070732e696f2f696d672f6f746865722d69636f6e732f72617370626572727970692d69636f6e2e737667"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/a3e0767e9f766cbaf33956f988f77b971bd6ae1af5f4b88592d683a34bb9f8b5/68747470733a2f2f70692d617070732e696f2f696d672f6f746865722d69636f6e732f72617370626572727970692d69636f6e2e737667" height="14" data-canonical-src="https://pi-apps.io/img/other-icons/raspberrypi-icon.svg" style="max-width: 100%;"></a> (2 v1.2/3/Zero 2 W/4/5)</h4><a id="user-content-raspberry-pi--2-v123zero-2-w45" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Raspberry Pi  (2 v1.2/3/Zero 2 W/4/5)" href="#raspberry-pi--2-v123zero-2-w45"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Unsupported systems:</h3><a id="user-content-unsupported-systems" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Unsupported systems:" href="#unsupported-systems"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Raspberry Pi Pico: <span>These devices are microcontrollers and cannot run linux.</span></li>
<li>All <strong>UNOFFICIAL</strong> Debian and Ubuntu based releases (unless mentioned above): <span>Expect many apps to have issues.</span>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Examples: <strong>Orange Pi OS</strong>, <a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/14a3d9661636cc2a35c44848fe522dd633e4971656c890cb313ad8c850fb340e/68747470733a2f2f70692d617070732e696f2f696d672f6f746865722d69636f6e732f706f702d6f732e737667"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/14a3d9661636cc2a35c44848fe522dd633e4971656c890cb313ad8c850fb340e/68747470733a2f2f70692d617070732e696f2f696d672f6f746865722d69636f6e732f706f702d6f732e737667" height="14" data-canonical-src="https://pi-apps.io/img/other-icons/pop-os.svg" style="max-width: 100%;"></a> <a href="https://pop.system76.com/" rel="nofollow"><strong>Pop_OS!</strong></a>, <strong>Kali Linux</strong>, and <strong>ChromeOS Crostini</strong> Debian Container</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Anything Non-Debian and Non-Ubuntu: <span>Expect the majority of apps and the appstore to be broken.</span>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Examples: <strong>Slackware</strong>, <strong>RHEL</strong>, <strong>Fedora</strong>, <strong>SUSE</strong>, <strong>Arch Linux</strong>, <strong>Gentoo</strong>, <strong>Void Linux</strong>, <strong>NixOS</strong></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Anything not already mentioned: <span>Expect nothing to work.</span>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Examples: <strong>Microsoft Windows</strong>, <strong>MacOS</strong>, <strong>Android</strong>, and <strong>ChromeOS</strong></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<details>
<summary><b>To install Pi-Apps manually</b> if you prefer to see what happens under the hood</summary>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="git clone https://github.com/Botspot/pi-apps
~/pi-apps/install"><pre class="notranslate"><code>git clone https://github.com/Botspot/pi-apps
~/pi-apps/install
</code></pre></div>
</details>
<details>
<summary><b>To uninstall Pi-Apps</b></summary>
This will not uninstall any apps that you installed through Pi-Apps.
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="~/pi-apps/uninstall"><pre class="notranslate"><code>~/pi-apps/uninstall
</code></pre></div>
</details>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">To run Pi-Apps</h2><a id="user-content-to-run-pi-apps" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: To run Pi-Apps" href="#to-run-pi-apps"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>From the start menu: Accessories -&gt; Pi-Apps</li>
<li>Use the terminal command: <code>pi-apps</code></li>
<li>Run Pi-Apps from its directory: <code>~/pi-apps/gui</code></li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">To update Pi-Apps</h2><a id="user-content-to-update-pi-apps" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: To update Pi-Apps" href="#to-update-pi-apps"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Pi-apps will automatically check for updates on boot and display a notification to update.</li>
<li>To manually run the updater, use this command: <code>~/pi-apps/updater gui</code></li>
<li>It also supports a cli interface: <code>~/pi-apps/updater cli</code></li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">What do others say about Pi-Apps?</h2><a id="user-content-what-do-others-say-about-pi-apps" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: What do others say about Pi-Apps?" href="#what-do-others-say-about-pi-apps"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<blockquote>
<p dir="auto">Message from a <strong><a href="https://pi-top.com" rel="nofollow">pi-top</a></strong> employee: "Happy to say that I recommend pi-apps to almost every school I work with when they start using Raspberry Pi"</p>
</blockquote>
<blockquote>

I want to give the devs of Pi-Apps a big shout-out."</p>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Basic usage</h2><a id="user-content-basic-usage" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Basic usage" href="#basic-usage"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Pi-Apps is very easy to use.</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">This is the <strong>main window</strong>.<br>
<a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/Botspot/pi-apps/blob/master/icons/screenshots/main%20window.png?raw=true"><img src="/Botspot/pi-apps/raw/master/icons/screenshots/main%20window.png?raw=true" alt="main window" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/Botspot/pi-apps/blob/master/icons/screenshots/buttons/search.png?raw=true"><img src="/Botspot/pi-apps/raw/master/icons/screenshots/buttons/search.png?raw=true" alt="icon" style="max-width: 100%;"></a> Search for apps.</li>
<li><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/Botspot/pi-apps/blob/master/icons/screenshots/buttons/settings.png?raw=true"><img src="/Botspot/pi-apps/raw/master/icons/screenshots/buttons/settings.png?raw=true" alt="icon" style="max-width: 100%;"></a> Open pi-apps settings.</li>
<li>Click on a category to open it.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">Opening a category will reveal a <strong>list of apps</strong>:<br>
<a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/Botspot/pi-apps/blob/master/icons/screenshots/app%20list.png?raw=true"><img src="/Botspot/pi-apps/raw/master/icons/screenshots/app%20list.png?raw=true" alt="app list" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/Botspot/pi-apps/blob/master/icons/screenshots/buttons/back2.png?raw=true"><img src="/Botspot/pi-apps/raw/master/icons/screenshots/buttons/back2.png?raw=true" alt="icon" style="max-width: 100%;"></a> Go back to the main list of categories.</li>
<li>Click on an App name to see its details (see <strong>details window</strong> below)</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">On the right is the app <strong>details window</strong>:<br>
<a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/Botspot/pi-apps/blob/master/icons/screenshots/details%20window.png?raw=true"><img src="/Botspot/pi-apps/raw/master/icons/screenshots/details%20window.png?raw=true" alt="details" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/Botspot/pi-apps/blob/master/icons/screenshots/buttons/scripts.png?raw=true"><img src="/Botspot/pi-apps/raw/master/icons/screenshots/buttons/scripts.png?raw=true" alt="icon" style="max-width: 100%;"></a> View the shell-scripts responsible for installing or uninstalling the selected app.</li>
<li><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/Botspot/pi-apps/blob/master/icons/screenshots/buttons/edit.png?raw=true"><img src="/Botspot/pi-apps/raw/master/icons/screenshots/buttons/edit.png?raw=true" alt="icon" style="max-width: 100%;"></a> Modify the app's description, icons, or scripts. (This button is hidden unless you enable it in Settings)</li>
<li><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/Botspot/pi-apps/blob/master/icons/screenshots/buttons/install.png?raw=true"><img src="/Botspot/pi-apps/raw/master/icons/screenshots/buttons/install.png?raw=true" alt="icon" style="max-width: 100%;"></a> Install the selected app.</li>
<li><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/Botspot/pi-apps/blob/master/icons/screenshots/buttons/uninstall.png?raw=true"><img src="/Botspot/pi-apps/raw/master/icons/screenshots/buttons/uninstall.png?raw=true" alt="icon" style="max-width: 100%;"></a> Uninstall the selected app.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">If you install/uninstall an app, you will see the <strong>progress window</strong>, keep installing/uninstalling apps to add them to the queue:<br>
<a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/Botspot/pi-apps/blob/master/icons/screenshots/manage.png?raw=true"><img src="/Botspot/pi-apps/raw/master/icons/screenshots/manage.png?raw=true" alt="details" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">Pi-Apps Settings can be configured by launching Menu -&gt; Preferences -&gt; Pi-Apps Settings.<br>
<a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/Botspot/pi-apps/blob/master/icons/screenshots/settings.png?raw=true"><img src="/Botspot/pi-apps/raw/master/icons/screenshots/settings.png?raw=true" alt="settings" style="max-width: 100%;"></a><br>
In addition to changeable settings, this window also gives access to these tools:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/Botspot/pi-apps/blob/master/icons/screenshots/buttons/categories.png?raw=true"><img src="/Botspot/pi-apps/raw/master/icons/screenshots/buttons/categories.png?raw=true" alt="icon" style="max-width: 100%;"></a> Does that one app seem to be in the wrong category? With this button, you can change it.</li>
<li><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/Botspot/pi-apps/blob/master/icons/screenshots/buttons/new%20app.png?raw=true"><img src="/Botspot/pi-apps/raw/master/icons/screenshots/buttons/new%20app.png?raw=true" alt="icon" style="max-width: 100%;"></a> Create a new app with a wizard-style set of dialogs. We recommend reading <a href="https://pi-apps.io/wiki/development/Creating-an-app/" rel="nofollow">the tutorial</a>.</li>
<li><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/Botspot/pi-apps/blob/master/icons/screenshots/buttons/log%20files.png?raw=true"><img src="/Botspot/pi-apps/raw/master/icons/screenshots/buttons/log%20files.png?raw=true" alt="icon" style="max-width: 100%;"></a> View the past weeks-worth of installation logs. This is useful if you ever encounter an app that won't install and want to see the terminal output after you closed the terminal.</li>
<li><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/Botspot/pi-apps/blob/master/icons/screenshots/buttons/import%20app.png?raw=true"><img src="/Botspot/pi-apps/raw/master/icons/screenshots/buttons/import%20app.png?raw=true" alt="icon" style="max-width: 100%;"></a> This allows you to easily import a 3rd-party app from elsewhere. It helps Pi-Apps developers test upcoming apps for reliability on a variety of systems.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">To learn more about Pi-Apps, read <a href="https://pi-apps.io/wiki/development/DOCUMENTATION/" rel="nofollow">the documentation</a> and the <a href="https://pi-apps.io/wiki/" rel="nofollow">wiki</a>.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto"> Contributing</h2><a id="user-content-raised_hands-contributing" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: :raised_hands: Contributing" href="#raised_hands-contributing"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">You don't need to be a programmer to help!</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>The easiest way to help is by "Starring" our repository - it helps more people find Pi-Apps. (Scroll to the top of this page and on the right there is a "Star" button)</li>
<li>If you know somebody else who has a Raspberry Pi, feel free to tell them about Pi-Apps. We would offer you a referral discount, but Pi-Apps is free, so... <code>\_()_/</code></li>
<li>You can <a href="https://github.com/Botspot/pi-apps/issues/new?template=suggestion.yml">make suggestions</a>, <a href="https://github.com/Botspot/pi-apps/issues/new?template=bug-report.yml">report bugs</a>, or <a href="https://github.com/Botspot/pi-apps/issues/new?template=app-suggestion.yml">suggest apps</a>.</li>
<li>You can <a href="https://pi-apps.io/wiki/development/Creating-an-app/" rel="nofollow">create and submit an app</a>. Don't worry, it's about as easy as using the terminal (and it's even easier if you're submitting a simple apt-package)!</li>
<li>You can also join our cheerful community: <a href="https://discord.gg/RXSTvaUvuu" rel="nofollow"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/cb6bf69120b8ae181a907e0c90ea30042596a00d351094ca6191874d44ca6a69/68747470733a2f2f696d672e736869656c64732e696f2f646973636f72642f3737303632393639373930393432343135392e7376673f636f6c6f723d373238396461266c6162656c3d446973636f7264253230736572766572266c6f676f3d646973636f7264" alt="Join the Discord server" data-canonical-src="https://img.shields.io/discord/770629697909424159.svg?color=7289da&amp;label=Discord%20server&amp;logo=discord" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Badge</h2><a id="user-content-badge" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Badge" href="#badge"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">If your application is on Pi-Apps, please consider adding this pretty badge/hyperlink to your README (dark and light modes available):</p>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/Botspot/pi-apps"><img src="https://github.com/Botspot/pi-apps/raw/master/icons/badge.png?raw=true" alt="badge" style="max-width: 100%;"></a>  <a href="https://github.com/Botspot/pi-apps"><img src="https://github.com/Botspot/pi-apps/raw/master/icons/badge-light.png?raw=true" alt="badge" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">Embed code (Dark):</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="[![badge](https://github.com/Botspot/pi-apps/blob/master/icons/badge.png?raw=true)](https://github.com/Botspot/pi-apps)"><pre class="notranslate"><code>[![badge](https://github.com/Botspot/pi-apps/blob/master/icons/badge.png?raw=true)](https://github.com/Botspot/pi-apps)
</code></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">Embed code (Light):</p>

</code></pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Q&amp;A with Botspot</h3><a id="user-content-qa-with-botspot" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Q&amp;A with Botspot" href="#qa-with-botspot"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Why did you make Pi-Apps?</li>
</ul>
<blockquote>
<p dir="auto">For a long time I have been saddened by how difficult it is to install software on Linux. In that regard, nearly all other operating systems put us to shame.<br>
How will people discover useful, free software?<br>
Most people <strong>don't</strong>.<br>
One day I realized: Why not make a collection of scripts to install popular apps? This would save so much time, and makes it much easier to use a Raspberry Pi as a daily, desktop computer solution.</p>
</blockquote>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>How long did it take to program this?</li>
</ul>
<blockquote>
<p dir="auto">Why would you think it's not still under development? <br>
Pi-Apps took around 14 days to lay the groundwork, and ever since then it has been continually, and exponentially, improved. I (Botspot) am not the sole programmer anymore - <a href="https://github.com/Botspot/pi-apps/graphs/contributors">others</a> have stepped in and made improvements too.</p>
</blockquote>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Is Pi-Apps free?</li>
</ul>
<blockquote>
<p dir="auto">Absolutely! <a href="https://github.com/sponsors/botspot">Donations are welcome</a>, but Pi-Apps itself will always be free and open-source.</p>
</blockquote>
